<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Parent Group</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 8.03</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Parent Indemnified Taxes</font>&#8221; means (i) all Tax liabilities attributable to the ownership, management and operation of the Acquired Companies or the ownership and operation of the Phase 1(a) Assets or the Business and incurred on or prior to the Execution Date or the ownership and operation of the Phase 1(b) Assets or the Phase 2 Assets and incurred on or prior to Phase 1(b) Closing Date or the Phase 2 Closing Date, as applicable, including (a) any such Tax liabilities of Parent and its Affiliates (including the Acquired Companies and the Purchaser) that may result from the consummation of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement, (b) any such Tax liabilities arising under Treasury Regulations Section 1.1502-6 and any similar provisions of state, local or foreign Law, by contract, as successor, transferee or otherwise, or which are attributable to having been a member of a consolidated, combined or unitary group, and (c) any Tax imposed on the Acquired Companies or the Purchaser that results from the business or operation of any other Affiliate of Parent, (ii) any payment required to be made following the applicable Closing as the result of the reduction, disallowance, preclusion of the availability, or recapture of any Cash Grant claimed or received with respect to a Project prior to the applicable Closing, and (iii) all Tax liabilities resulting from any reduction, disallowance, preclusion of the availability, or recapture under Section 50 of the Code of tax credits claimed, allowed, or allowable with respect to a Project or allocated by the Acquired Companies prior to the applicable Closing; <font style="text-decoration:underline;">provided</font>, <font style="text-decoration:underline;">however</font>, that the Parties hereby agree that in no event shall any payment, liability or other Damages whatsoever arising as the result of, or that otherwise would not have been incurred except through, any action of an 8point3 Entity following the applicable Closing be deemed to constitute Parent Indemnified Taxes.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Parent Material Adverse Effect</font>&#8221; means a Material Adverse Effect with respect to the Acquired Companies, the Phase 1(a) Assets, the Phase 1(b) Assets and the Phase 2 Assets, taken as a whole, or a material adverse effect on the ability of Parent or its Affiliates to consummate </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">10</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">the transactions contemplated by the Transaction Documents or to perform its material obligations under the Transaction Documents to which such Person is a party.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Parent Party</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 4.01</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Parent Specified Representations</font>&#8221; means those representations and warranties made in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Sections 4.01</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">Organization; Qualification</font>), 4.02 (<font style="font-style:italic;">Authority and Power</font>), <font style="text-decoration:underline;">4.03</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">Valid and Binding Obligation</font>), <font style="text-decoration:underline;">4.06</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">Transfer of Company Interests</font>), <font style="text-decoration:underline;">4.07</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">Capital Stock</font>), 4.11<font style="text-decoration:underline;">(b)</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">Personal Property; Sufficiency of Assets</font>) and <font style="text-decoration:underline;">4.21</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">No Brokers</font>).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Partnership</font>&#8221; means 8point3 Energy Partners LP, a Delaware limited partnership.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Partnership Agreement</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Recitals.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Party</font>&#8221; or &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Parties</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Preamble.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Payment Request</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Master Purchase Agreement.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Permits</font>&#8221; means written permits, licenses, certificates, franchises, registrations, exemptions, authorizations, variances, consents and approvals obtained from any Governmental Entity.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Permitted Equity Liens</font>&#8221; means (a) restrictions on transfer imposed by applicable securities Laws, (b) with respect to the Company Interests, restrictions on transfer set forth in the Charter Documents of the Company, (c) with respect to the Equity Interests in Intermediate Holding Company, restrictions on transfer set forth in the Charter Documents of Intermediate Holding Company, (d) with respect to the Equity Interests in the Project Company, restrictions on transfer set forth in the Charter Documents of such Project Company, (e) Liens that arise as the result of any Tax Equity Financing and (f) those matters set forth in Part I of <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Schedule 1.1(b)</font> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Permitted Liens</font>&#8221; means (a) Liens for Taxes not yet due and payable or for Taxes being contested in good faith through appropriate proceedings and for which in each case appropriate reserves in accordance with GAAP have been recorded on the Balance Sheet; (b) mechanics&#8217;, materialmens&#8217; or other similar Liens arising in the ordinary course of business for sums that are not yet due and payable or for which adequate reserves have been taken on the Balance Sheet; (c) other Liens arising in the ordinary course of business for sums that are immaterial in amount to the Acquired Companies and not yet due and payable and do not materially detract from the value of or materially impair the existing or contemplated use of the property affected by such Lien; (d) zoning, entitlement, conservation restriction and other land use and environmental regulations by Governmental Entities that do not, in each case, materially detract from the value or materially impair the existing or contemplated use of the land or other property affected by such restrictions or regulations; (e) any matters of record that are not material in amount to the affected Acquired Company and do not materially detract from the value of or materially impair or inhibit the existing or contemplated use or operation of the property affected by such Lien; (f) customary set-off and similar netting arrangements in favor of banks in connection with deposit accounts, security accounts and similar banking arrangements arising in the ordinary course of </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">11</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">business; (g) those matters set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Schedule 1.1(c)</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule and (h) any Permitted Equity Lien.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Person</font>&#8221; means an individual or a corporation, firm, limited liability company, partnership, joint venture, trust, estate, unincorporated organization, association, Governmental Entity or political subdivision thereof or other entity.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(a) Assets</font>&#8221; means all equipment, facilities and other tangible and intangible assets and rights substantially used by or held for use by the Project Company or the Project Development Company in connection with the Initial Project Sites.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(a) Closing</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.01(a)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(a) Purchase Price</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.01(b)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Assets</font>&#8221; means all equipment, facilities and other tangible and intangible assets and rights substantially used by or held for use by the Project Development Company in connection with the Development Project Sites, other than those included in the Phase 1(a) Assets, that Parent determines will be sold, transferred and assigned to the Project Company as part of the Phase 1(b) Closing, including all of the assets listed under the name of such Development Project Sites on <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Schedule B</font> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Closing</font>&#8221; means the closing of the acquisition of the Phase 1(b) Assets pursuant to the Master Purchase Agreement.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Closing Certificate</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.02(b)(i)(3)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Contribution</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.02(a)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Contribution Amount</font>&#8221; means the amount calculated by multiplying (i) the aggregate numerical amount of the MWac of the Development Project Sites included in the Phase 1(b) Assets by (ii) $1,729,805.71.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.01(b)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.01(b)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Assets</font>&#8221; means (i) all equipment, facilities and other tangible and intangible assets and rights substantially used by or held for use by the Project Development Company in connection with the Development Project Sites, other than those included in the Phase 1(a) Assets or the Phase 1(b) Assets, that Parent determines will be sold, transferred and assigned to the Project Company as part of the Phase 2 Closing, including all of the assets listed under the name of such Development Project Sites on <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Schedule B</font> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, and (ii) all other equipment, facilities and other tangible and intangible assets and rights solely used by or held for use by the Project Development Company in connection with the Project and not otherwise previously assigned to the Project Company.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">12</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Closing</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8221; means the closing of the acquisition of the Phase 2 Assets pursuant to the Master Purchase Agreement.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Closing Certificate</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.02(c)(i)(3)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Contribution</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.02(b)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Contribution Amount</font>&#8221; means the amount calculated by subtracting the Phase 1(a) Purchase Price and the Phase 1(b) Contribution Amount from the Purchase Price.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Contribution Closing</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.01(c)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.01(c)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Plan</font>&#8221; means any bonus, incentive compensation, deferred compensation, pension, profit sharing, retirement, stock purchase, stock option, stock ownership, stock appreciation rights, restricted stock, phantom stock, stock or cash award, deferred compensation, leave of absence, layoff, stay, vacation, day or dependent care, legal services, cafeteria, life, health, welfare, post-retirement, accident, disability, worker&#8217;s compensation or other insurance, severance, separation, change of control, employment or other employee benefit plan, practice, policy, agreement or arrangement of any kind, whether written or oral, or whether for the benefit of a single individual or more than one individual including any &#8220;employee benefit plan&#8221; within the meaning of Section 3(3) of ERISA.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Pledge and Security Agreement</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Credit Agreement.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Project</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Recitals.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Project Company</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Recitals.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Project Development Company</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Recitals.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Project Model</font>&#8221; means the financial model for the Project, as transmitted by email from Natalie Jackson to Thomas O&#8217;Connor, on January 25, 2016 at 1:22 p.m. (Pacific time).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Project Permits</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 4.14(a)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Project Tax Credit</font>&#8221; means the investment tax credit under Section 48 of the Code and the production tax credit under Section 45 of the Code.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Prudent Solar Industry Practice</font>&#8221; means those practices, methods, and acts that a nationally recognized owner, developer or operator of projects of good standing, at a particular time, in the exercise of prudent judgment in light of the facts known or that reasonably should have been known at the time a decision was made, would have taken to accomplish the desired result in a manner consistent with law, regulation, permits, codes, standards, equipment manufacturer&#8217;s recommendations, reliability, safety, environmental protection, economy, and expedition. &#8220;Prudent Solar Industry Practice&#8221; does not necessarily mean the best practice, </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">13</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">method, or standard of care, skill, safety and diligence in all cases, but is instead intended to encompass a range of acceptable practices, methods and standards.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">PUHCA</font>&#8221; means the Public Utility Holding Company Act of 2005, and FERC&#8217;s regulations and orders thereunder.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Purchase Price</font>&#8221; means an amount in cash equal to $35,000,000 (Thirty-Five Million Dollars).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Purchaser</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Preamble.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Purchaser Group</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 8.02</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Purchaser Material Adverse Effect</font>&#8221; means a Material Adverse Effect on the ability of Purchaser or its Affiliates to consummate the transactions contemplated by the Transaction Documents or to perform its obligations under the Transaction Documents to which Purchaser or its Affiliates is a party.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Purchaser Specified Representations</font>&#8221; means those representations and warranties made in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Sections 5.01</font> (<font style="font-style:italic;">Organization; Qualification</font>), 5.02 (<font style="font-style:italic;">Authority and Power</font>), 5.03 (<font style="font-style:italic;">Valid and Binding Obligation</font>) and 5.06 (<font style="font-style:italic;">No Brokers</font>).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Real Property Interests</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 4.10(d)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Recoveries</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 8.06(d)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Release</font>&#8221; means any depositing, spilling, leaking, pumping, pouring, placing, emitting, discarding, abandoning, emptying, discharging, migrating, injecting, escaping, leaching, dumping, or disposing into the indoor or outdoor environment (including soil, ambient air, surface water, groundwater and surface or subsurface strata) or into or out of any property, including the movement of Hazardous Substances through or in the air, soil, surface water, groundwater or property.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Representatives</font>&#8221; means, with respect to any Person, such Person&#8217;s directors, officers, employees, agents and other representatives, including legal counsel, accountants and consultants.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">ROFO Agreement</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 11.14</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Schedule Update</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.06(a)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Securities Act</font>&#8221; means the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, supplemented or restated from time to time, and any successor to such statute.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Specified Affiliate Bonuses</font>&#8221; means any &#8220;Performance Bonus,&#8221; &#8220;Bonus Payment&#8221; or any similar bonus, to the extent paid to Parent or any Affiliate thereof (including SunPower Corporation, Systems), in its role as operator or contractor under any performance guarantee agreement, engineering, procurement and construction contract, or similar agreement, entered </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">14</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">into between Parent or its Affiliate, as operator or contractor, and any Acquired Company</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">, directly or indirectly,</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> by Parent or any Affiliate thereof.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Specified Representations</font>&#8221; means each of the Parent Specified Representations and the Purchaser Specified Representations, as the context may require.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Subsidiary</font>&#8221; means, with respect to any Person, (a)&#160;a corporation of which more than 50% of the voting power of shares entitled (without regard to the occurrence of any contingency) to vote in the election of directors or other governing body of such corporation is owned, directly or indirectly, at the date of determination, by such Person, by one or more Subsidiaries of such Person or a combination thereof, (b)&#160;a partnership (whether general or limited) in which such Person or a Subsidiary of such Person is, at the date of determination, a general or limited partner of such partnership, but only if such Person, one or more Subsidiaries of such Person, or a combination thereof, controls such partnership on the date of hereof, or (c)&#160;any other Person (other than a corporation or a partnership) in which such Person, directly or by one or more Subsidiaries of such Person, or a combination thereof, directly or indirectly, at the date of determination, (i) has the power to elect or direct the election of a majority of the directors or other governing body of such Person or (ii) is a managing member or sole or controlling member.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">SunPower Capital</font>&#8221; means SunPower Capital Services, LLC, a Delaware limited liability company.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax</font>&#8221; or &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Taxes</font>&#8221; shall mean any federal, state, local or foreign taxes and other taxes, charges, fees, duties, levies or other assessments, imposts, deductions, withholdings, including income, gross receipts, license, payroll, employment, excise, severance, stamp, occupation, premium, windfall profits, environmental, customs duties, capital stock, franchise, profits, withholding, social security, unemployment, disability, real property, personal property, sales, use, transfer, registration, value added, alternative or add-on minimum, estimated, leasing, fuel, and utility taxes, unclaimed property or escheat obligations, or other governmental charges of any kind whatsoever, that are imposed by any Governmental Entity of any country or political subdivision of any country, including any interest, penalty or addition thereto, whether disputed or not.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax Equity Breach</font>&#8221; means the occurrence of any event resulting in an Indemnifiable Tax Equity Payment with respect to the Acquired Companies.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax Equity Financing</font>&#8221; means those transactions described in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Schedule 1.1(d)</font> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax Equity Funds Flow</font>&#8221; means the Funds Flow Memorandum (as defined in the Master Purchase Agreement) required to be provided to the Intermediate Holding Company pursuant to Section 4.1(c)(xxx) of the Master Purchase Agreement.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax Equity Investor</font>&#8221; means Wells Fargo Wind Holdings LLC.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax Equity Purchase Shortfall</font>&#8221; means the difference of (a) the purchase price payable by any member of the Purchaser Group to Parent or any Affiliate thereof in respect of the </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">15</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">acquisition of any Acquired Company, any Phase 1(a) Asset, any Acquired Asset or the Project less (b) the aggregate amount of (i) all proceeds received by the Purchaser Group pursuant to the Tax Equity Financing in respect of the Acquired Companies, any Phase 1(a) Asset, the Acquired Asset or the Project and (ii) all equity contribution proceeds received by the Purchaser Group from, or on behalf of, Parent or any Affiliate thereof, in each case, to the extent such Tax Equity Financing proceeds and equity contribution proceeds were contemplated to fund the payment of such purchase price.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tax Returns</font>&#8221; means any return, report, declaration, information return, statement, property Tax rendition, or other document filed or required to be filed with any Governmental Entity (including any schedule, appendix or attachment thereto, and including any amendment thereof) in connection with the determination, assessment or collection of any Tax or the administration of any Laws, regulations or administrative requirements relating to any Tax.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Termination Date</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 9.01(c)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Third Party Claim</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 8.05(a)</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Tranche Presentation Certificate</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in the Master Purchase Agreement.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Transaction Documents</font>&#8221; means this Agreement, the Assignment and Assumption Agreement, the Amended and Restated Company LLC Agreement and the Bills of Sale.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Transfer Taxes</font>&#8221; has the meaning set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 10.06</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Treasury Regulations</font>&#8221; means the regulations (including temporary regulations) promulgated by the United States Department of the Treasury pursuant to and in respect of provisions of the Code.&nbsp;&nbsp;All references herein to sections of the Treasury Regulations shall include any corresponding provision or provisions of succeeding, similar or substitute, temporary or final Treasury Regulations.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700859"></a>1.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Construction; Interpretation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except where expressly provided or unless the contract otherwise necessarily requires, in this Agreement:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052640"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Reference to a given Article, Section, clause or Exhibit is a reference to an Article, Section, clause or Exhibit of this Agreement, unless otherwise specified.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Exhibits and Schedules attached to this Agreement are hereby incorporated by reference into this Agreement and form part hereof.&nbsp;&nbsp;The terms &#8220;hereof&#8221;, &#8220;herein&#8221;, &#8220;hereunder&#8221; and &#8220;herewith&#8221; refer to this Agreement as a whole (including the Parent Disclosure Schedule, the Exhibits and Schedules).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052641"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Parent Disclosure Schedule sets forth items of disclosure with specific reference to the particular Section or subsection of this Agreement to which the information in the Parent Disclosure Schedule relates; </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">provided</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, that any fact or item that is disclosed in any section of the Parent Disclosure Schedule that is reasonably apparent on its face, upon a reading of the disclosure together with the corresponding representation or warranty and without any independent knowledge on the part of the reader regarding the matter disclosed, to qualify </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">16</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">another representation or warranty of Parent shall be deemed also to be disclosed in the other sections of the Parent Disclosure Schedule notwithstanding the omission of any appropriate cross-reference thereto.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding anything in this Agreement to the contrary, the inclusion of an item in a disclosure schedule as an exception to a representation or warranty will not be deemed an admission that such item represents a material exception or material fact, event or circumstance or that such item has had or could reasonably be expected to have a Parent Material Adverse Effect.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052642"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Unless otherwise specifically indicated or the context otherwise requires, (i) all references to &#8220;dollars&#8221; or &#8220;$&#8221; mean United States dollars, (ii) words importing the singular shall include the plural and vice versa, and words importing any gender shall include all genders, (iii) all references to &#8220;days&#8221; means calendar days, (iv) &#8220;include,&#8221; &#8220;includes&#8221; and &#8220;including&#8221; shall be deemed to be followed by the words &#8220;without limitation,&#8221; and (v) all words used as accounting terms shall have the meanings assigned to them under GAAP applied on a consistent basis and as amended from time to time.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052643"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">If any date on which any action is required to be taken hereunder by any of the Parties hereto is not a Business Day, such action shall be required to be taken on the next succeeding day that is a Business Day.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052644"></a>(e)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Reference to a given agreement, instrument, document or Law is a reference to that agreement, instrument, document or Law as modified, amended, supplemented and restated through the date as of which such reference is made, and, as to any Law, any successor Law.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052645"></a>(f)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Reference to a Person includes its predecessors, successors and permitted assigns.&nbsp;&nbsp;Any reference to any federal, state, local, or foreign Law shall be deemed also to refer to all rules and regulations promulgated thereunder, unless the context requires otherwise.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052646"></a>(g)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The word &#8220;will&#8221; shall be construed to have the same meaning and effect as the word &#8220;shall.&#8221;&nbsp;&nbsp;The word &#8220;or&#8221; shall not be exclusive.</font></p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052648"></a>(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">No provision of this Agreement will be interpreted in favor of, or against, any of the Parties to this Agreement by reason of the extent to which any such Party or its counsel participated in the drafting thereof or by reason of the extent to which any such provision is inconsistent with any prior draft of this Agreement, and no rule of strict construction will be applied against any Party hereto.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052649"></a>(j)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The term &#8220;made available&#8221; and words of similar import means that the relevant documents, instruments or materials were posted and made available to the other Party on the SunPower Corporation ShareFile due diligence data site maintained by the Parent for the purpose of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement, prior to the date hereof.</font></p>

<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700860"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ARTICLE II</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;">PURCHASE AND SALE OF COMPANY INTERESTS; CONTRIBUTIONS</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439128919"></a><a name="_Toc439700861"></a><a name="_Ref440655413"></a>2.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Purchase and Sale of Company Interests</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="_Ref440655413"></a>.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref440656509"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">On the terms and conditions set forth herein, on the Execution Date, Parent hereby agrees to cause AssetCo to sell, transfer and assign to 8point3 OpCo Holdings, and Purchaser hereby agrees to cause 8point3 OpCo Holdings to purchase, assume and accept from AssetCo, free and clear of all Liens, other than Permitted Equity Liens, the Company Interests (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Company Interest Acquisition</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref440655584"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The aggregate consideration for the Company Interest Acquisition is $4,887,573.96 in cash (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(a) Purchase Price</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref440655872"></a>2.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Contributions</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="_Ref440655872"></a>.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref441097063"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(b) Contribution</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;On the terms and conditions set forth herein, on the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date, Purchaser hereby agrees to cause 8point3 OpCo Holdings to contribute the Phase 1(b) Contribution Amount as a contribution of capital to the Company, and the Company shall accept such contribution of capital (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(b) Contribution</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref440655886"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 2 Contribution</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;On the terms and conditions set forth herein, on the Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date, Purchaser hereby agrees to cause 8point3 OpCo Holdings to contribute the Phase 2 Contribution Amount as a contribution of capital to the Company, and the Company shall accept such contribution of capital (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 2 Contribution</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ARTICLE III<font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br><br>CLOSINGS</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">3.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Closings</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439944073"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(a) Closing Date</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;The closing of the Company Interest Acquisition (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(a) Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) shall be held on the Execution Date and shall occur simultaneously with the execution of this Agreement by the Parties.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439944109"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the terms and conditions set forth herein, the closing of the Phase 1(b) Contribution (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) shall be held on the &#8220;Initial Funding Date&#8221; set forth in the Payment Request for the Phase 1(b) Assets; </font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">provided</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> that the Tranche Presentation Certificate for the Phase 1(b) Assets represented that the Development Project Sites which achieved mechanical completion and which are to be included in the closing under the Master Purchase Agreement with respect to the Phase 1(b) Assets equaled at least an aggregate of 1 MWac (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).&nbsp;&nbsp;On the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date and simultaneous with the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing, the closing under the Master Purchase Agreement shall occur with respect to the Phase 1(b) Assets.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">18</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439944019"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(c)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Subject to the terms and conditions set forth herein, the closing of the Phase 2 Contribution (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 2 Contribution Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221; and, together with the Phase 1(a) Closing and the Phase 1(b) Closing, each a &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) shall be held on the &#8220;Initial Funding Date&#8221; set forth in the Payment Request for the Phase 2 Assets; provided that the Tranche Presentation Certificate for the Phase 2 Assets represented that all remaining Development Project Sites achieved mechanical completion (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221; and, together with the Execution Date and the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date, each a &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Closing Date</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).&nbsp;&nbsp;On the Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date and simultaneous with the Phase 2 Contribution Closing, the closing under the Master Purchase Agreement shall occur with respect to the Phase 2 Assets.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439944003"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Closing Time and Place</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Closing shall be held at the offices of Baker Botts L.L.P., 910 Louisiana Street, Houston Texas 77002, at 10:00 a.m., local time on the respective Closing Date.</font></p>
