<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Parent hereby represents and warrants to Purchaser as follows as of the Execution Date:</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129366"></a><a name="_Ref439129374"></a><a name="_Toc439700865"></a>4.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Organization; Qualification</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052663"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each of Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company and the Acquired Companies (each, a &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent Party</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) has been duly formed and is validly existing and in good standing as a corporation or limited liability company, as applicable, under the Laws of its jurisdiction of formation</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">with all requisite corporate or limited liability company, as applicable, power and authority to own, lease or otherwise hold and operate its properties and assets and to carry on its business as presently conducted; except, in the case of Parent, AssetCo and the Project Development Company, where the failure to have such power and authority would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Parent Material Adverse Effect.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">21</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052664"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each Parent Party is duly qualified and in good standing to do business as a foreign corporation or foreign limited liability company, as the case may be, in each jurisdiction in which the conduct or nature of its business or the ownership, leasing, holding or operating of its properties makes such qualification necessary, except such jurisdictions where the failure to be so qualified or in good standing would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Parent Material Adverse Effect.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052665"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent has heretofore made available, or has caused to be made available, to Purchaser complete and correct copies of the Charter Documents of each Acquired Company.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129382"></a><a name="_Toc439700866"></a>4.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Authority and Power</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Each Parent Party (a) has all requisite corporate or limited liability company, as applicable, power and authority to execute and deliver each of the Transaction Documents to which it is a party, to perform its obligations hereunder and thereunder, and to consummate the transactions contemplated hereby and thereby, and (b) has taken all necessary corporate or limited liability company, as applicable, action to authorize the execution, delivery and performance of the Transaction Documents to which it is a party.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129389"></a><a name="_Toc439700867"></a>4.03<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Valid and Binding Obligation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052668"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">This Agreement has been duly and validly executed and delivered by Parent and, assuming this Agreement has been duly and validly authorized, executed and delivered by Purchaser, constitutes a legal, valid and binding obligation of Parent, enforceable against Parent in accordance with its terms, except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, insolvency, fraudulent transfer, reorganization, moratorium or similar Laws relating to or affecting the enforcement of creditors&#8217; rights in general and by general principles of equity.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052669"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each of the Transaction Documents to which Parent, AssetCo or the Project Development Company is a party will be duly and validly executed and delivered by Parent, AssetCo or the Project Development Company, as applicable, and, upon execution and delivery thereof, and assuming such Transaction Document has been duly and validly authorized, executed and delivered by Purchaser and any Affiliates of Purchaser party thereto, will constitute a legal, valid and binding obligation of Parent, AssetCo or the Project Development Company, as applicable, enforceable against Parent, AssetCo or the Project Development Company, as applicable, in accordance with its terms, except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, insolvency, fraudulent transfer, reorganization, moratorium or similar Laws relating to or affecting the enforcement of creditors&#8217; rights in general and by general principles of equity.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439128980"></a><a name="_Toc439700868"></a>4.04<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">No Violation or Conflict</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.05</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, none of the execution, delivery or performance of the Transaction Documents by each Parent Party, nor the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby or thereby, will (a) conflict with or violate any provision of the Charter Documents of any Parent Party, (b) constitute, with or without notice or the passage of time or both, a material violation, a material breach or default, create a material Lien, conflict in any material respect with, or require any material consent or approval, or give rise to any material right of termination, modification, cancellation, prepayment, suspension, limitation, revocation, preemption, right of first refusal (or similar right to purchase) or acceleration (any or all of the foregoing, a &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Default</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) under any </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">22</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">material Permit or Contract to which any Parent Party is a party or by which any of their respective properties are bound or (c) contravene, in any material respect, any material Law. </font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700869"></a><a name="_Ref439971849"></a>4.05<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Consents and Approvals</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.05</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule sets forth each material Consent of, with or to any Governmental Entity or other Person that is required to be obtained or made by or with respect to any Parent Party in connection with (i) the execution and delivery of this Agreement and the other Transaction Documents, or (ii) the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby or thereby and each such Consent has been obtained, waived or the time for asserting such right has expired.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129399"></a><a name="_Toc439700870"></a>4.06<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Transfer of </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Company </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Interests</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. AssetCo is the record and beneficial direct owner of and holds good, valid and transferable title to the Company Interests.&nbsp;&nbsp;The delivery by AssetCo of the Assignment and Assumption Agreement, duly executed by AssetCo and 8point3 OpCo Holdings, will transfer to 8point3 OpCo Holdings good and valid title to the Company Interests free and clear of any Liens (other than Permitted Equity Liens), and admit 8point3 OpCo Holdings as the sole class B member of, the Company, immediately upon the Phase 1(a) Closing.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700871"></a>4.07<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Capital Stock</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052674"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Other than Intermediate Holding Company and the Project Company, the Company has no Subsidiaries and does not own, directly or indirectly, any Equity Interests in any corporation, partnership, limited liability company or other Person.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except for Permitted Equity Liens and as otherwise set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no outstanding Liens relating to the Company Interests, and no outstanding rights, options, warrants, rights of first refusal, calls, preemptive rights, conversion rights, subscriptions, commitments, arrangements or other agreements pursuant to which AssetCo or the Company is, or may be, obligated to sell, issue or acquire any Company Interests.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, no Company Interests are represented by any certificate or other instrument.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052675"></a><a name="_Toc438052676"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Other than the Project Company, Intermediate Holding Company has no Subsidiaries and does not own, directly or indirectly, any Equity Interests in any corporation, partnership, limited liability company or other Person.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except for Permitted Equity Liens and as otherwise set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no outstanding Liens relating to the Equity Interests in Intermediate Holding Company (other than Liens on those Equity Interests not owned by the Company), and no outstanding rights, options, warrants, rights of first refusal, calls, preemptive rights, conversion rights, subscriptions, commitments, arrangements or other agreements pursuant to which the Company or Intermediate Holding Company is, or may be, obligated to sell, issue or acquire any Equity Interests in Intermediate Holding Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, no Equity Interests in Intermediate Holding Company are represented by any certificate or other instrument.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Project Company has no Subsidiaries and does not own, directly or indirectly, any Equity Interests in any corporation, partnership, limited liability company or other Person.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except for Permitted Equity Liens and as otherwise set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no outstanding Liens relating to the Equity Interests in the Project Company, and no outstanding rights, options, warrants, rights of first refusal, calls, </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">23</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">preemptive rights, conversion rights, subscriptions, commitments, arrangements or other agreements pursuant to which Intermediate Holding Company or the Project Company is, or may be, obligated to sell, issue or acquire any Equity Interests in the Project Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, no Equity Interests in the Project Company are represented by any certificate or other instrument.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052677"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Company Interests are not subject to any voting trust, member or partnership agreement or voting agreement or other agreement, right, instrument or understanding with respect to any purchase, sale, issuance, transfer, repurchase, redemption or voting of the Company Interests, other than those contained in the Charter Documents thereof or otherwise set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company Interests were duly authorized, validly issued, fully paid and nonassessable and were not issued in violation of any preemptive rights, rights of first refusal or similar rights and AssetCo is the sole member of the Company immediately prior to the Phase 1(a) Closing.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052678"></a><a name="_Toc438052679"></a>(e)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Equity Interests in Intermediate Holding Company (other than such Equity Interests not directly or indirectly owned by the Company) are not subject to any voting trust, member or partnership agreement or voting agreement or other agreement, right, instrument or understanding with respect to any purchase, sale, issuance, transfer, repurchase, redemption or voting of such Equity Interests, other than those contained in the Charter Documents thereof or otherwise set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Equity Interests in Intermediate Holding Company were duly authorized, validly issued, fully paid and nonassessable and were not issued in violation of any preemptive rights, rights of first refusal or similar rights and the Company, the Tax Equity Investor and SunPower Capital are the only members of Intermediate Holding Company immediately prior to the Phase 1(a) Closing.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(f)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Equity Interests in the Project Company are not subject to any voting trust, member or partnership agreement or voting agreement or other agreement, right, instrument or understanding with respect to any purchase, sale, issuance, transfer, repurchase, redemption or voting of such Equity Interests, other than those contained in the Charter Documents thereof or otherwise set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.07</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Equity Interests in the Project Company were duly authorized, validly issued, fully paid and nonassessable and were not issued in violation of any preemptive rights, rights of first refusal or similar rights and Intermediate Holding Company is the sole member of the Project Company immediately prior to the Phase 1(a) Closing.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700872"></a>4.08<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Financial Statements</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref436051863"></a><a name="_Toc438052681"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Attached hereto at </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.08(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule is a true and complete copy of the unaudited balance sheet of the Acquired Companies and the Project Development Company prepared on a consolidated basis as of January 3, 2016 (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Balance Sheet</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref436051864"></a><a name="_Toc438052682"></a><a name="DocXTextRef158"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="DocXTextRef158"></a>Except as set forth therein, the Balance Sheet (i) presents fairly in all material respects the consolidated financial position of the Acquired Companies and the Project Development Company, at the date set forth therein in accordance with GAAP applied on a </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">24</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">consistent basis throughout the periods covered thereby, except that the Balance Sheet has been prepared without footnotes and is subject to normal year-end adjustments, which are not expected to be material either individually or in the aggregate, and (ii) has been prepared from, is in accordance with and accurately reflects, the books and the accounting and financial records of the Acquired Companies and the Project Development Company covered by such Balance Sheet, which books and records are accurate and complete in all material respects.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700873"></a>4.09<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Undisclosed Liabilities</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except for (a) liabilities or obligations that are reflected on or reserved against on the Balance Sheet, to the extent so reflected or reserved thereon, (b) liabilities or obligations incurred in the ordinary course of business after the date of the most recent Balance Sheet, or (c) liabilities of the Acquired Companies and the Project Development Company that, individually or in the aggregate, are not material to the Acquired Companies or the Acquired Assets, taken as a whole, the Acquired Companies and the Project Development Company have no liabilities that would be required to be reflected on a balance sheet prepared in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700874"></a><a name="_Ref439971864"></a>4.10<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Real Property</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052686"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.10(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule sets forth a true, correct and complete list of the following:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129054"></a>(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">all real property owned in fee by (A) the Acquired Companies or (B) the Project Development Company which are included in the Acquired Assets (&#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Owned Real Property</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;); and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref440110554"></a>(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">all real property (A) leased or subleased to (I) the Acquired Companies or (II) the Project Development Company which are included in the Acquired Assets or (B) subject to other leasehold interests, easements, air rights and rights-of-way appertaining or related thereto, or other similar interest in real property in favor of (I) the Acquired Companies or (II) the Project Development Company which are included in the Acquired Assets (all such real property together with all buildings and other improvements thereon, &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Leased Real Property</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052687"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The agreements pursuant to which the Leased Real Property is leased by (i) the Project Company or (ii) the Project Development Company which are included in the Acquired Assets are, in each case, in full force and effect and enforceable against the Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company, as applicable, and to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, each other party thereto in accordance with their terms (except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, insolvency, reorganization, moratorium, or similar Laws relating to or affecting the enforcement of creditor&#8217;s rights in general and by general principles of equity) and there are no defaults by the Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company, as applicable, nor to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, any other party to such agreements, and the Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company, as applicable, have not received any notice of termination with respect to any such agreements.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">25</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052688"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(c)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company, as applicable, have good, marketable and indefeasible fee title to the Owned Real Property owned by it, subject to no Liens other than Permitted Liens.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company, as applicable, have a valid and subsisting leasehold or subleasehold estate in, and the right to make use of, the Leased Real Property subject to the terms and conditions of the applicable lease or sublease agreement and subject to no Liens other than Permitted Liens. No Acquired Company nor the Project Development Company has granted any assignment, lease, license, sublease, easement, concession, option or other agreement granting to any Person the right to possess, use, control, or occupy the Real Property Interests or any portion thereof except as would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to materially impair the use or operation of the Project.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052689"></a><a name="_Ref439129118"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">With respect to the Owned Real Property and Leased Real Property (collectively, the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Real Property Interests</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;), none of Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company, their Affiliates or any Acquired Company, has received any written notice of any material appropriation, condemnation or like proceeding, or of any material violation of any applicable zoning or land use law, regulation or rule or other law, order, regulation, rule or requirement relating to or affecting any of the Real Property Interests. </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052690"></a>(e)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as set forth in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.10(e)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of Parent Disclosure Schedule:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">there are no existing severed or other mineral rights affecting the Real Property Interests that, if exercised, could materially and adversely affect the development, construction, ownership, operation, use or management of the Project;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">neither Parent nor its Affiliates nor any Acquired Company has received any written notice of any mining, mineral or water extraction or development projects under construction or for which Permits are currently being obtained, located, or planned to be located on or under the properties constituting the Real Property Interest, or any portion thereof, which would materially and adversely affect the Project; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no portion of the Project encroaches on property outside the boundaries of the Real Property Interests without the written consent of the owner of that property. </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700875"></a>4.11<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Personal Property; Sufficiency of Assets</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052692"></a><a name="_Ref439128887"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Other than with respect to Intellectual Property, which is addressed in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.25</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, the Acquired Companies own and have good and marketable title to, or, in the case of leased assets, a valid and marketable leasehold interest in, or, in the case of licensed assets, a valid license to, the Phase 1(a) Assets, free and clear of any Liens, other than Permitted Liens.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439971876"></a><a name="_Toc438052693"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Other than with respect to Intellectual Property, which is addressed in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.25</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, the Project Development Company owns and has good and marketable title to, or, in the case of leased assets, a valid and marketable leasehold interest in, or, in the case of licensed assets, a valid license to, the Acquired Assets, free and clear of any Liens, other than </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">26</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Permitted Liens.</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;Following the Phase 1(b) Closing and the Phase 2 Closing, the Project Company will own and have good and marketable title to, or, in the case of leased assets, a valid and marketable leasehold interest in, or, in the case of licensed assets, a valid license to, the Phase 1(b) Assets or the Phase 2 Assets, as applicable, free and clear of any Liens, other than Permitted Liens.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439971884"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The tangible Phase 1(a) Assets and Acquired Assets have been maintained in accordance with Prudent Solar Industry Practices.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.11(c)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, and except for equipment, facilities and tangible personal property that is entitled to be repaired, replaced or otherwise remediated (to the extent that such repair, replacement or other remediation is reasonably expected to be less than $25,000) under an existing manufacturers&#8217; warranty or other contractual warranty which remains in effect, the tangible Phase 1(a) Assets and Acquired Assets that are material to the Project, taken as a whole, are in good repair and proper operating condition (ordinary wear and tear excepted).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052694"></a><a name="_Ref439971890"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as set forth on Part I of </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.11(d)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no written force majeure claims or, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, no delays in completing the Project that are reasonably likely to result in the Commercial Operation Date for the solar generation systems (i) held by the Project Company at the Phase 1(a) Closing, (ii) within the Phase 1(b) Assets or (iii) within the Phase 2 Assets, failing to occur prior to the date set forth therefor on Part II of </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.11(d)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of Parent Disclosure Schedule or in a Parent Material Adverse Effect.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(e)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Phase 1(a) Assets, Acquired Assets and the Real Property Interests, taken as a whole, constitute all of the material assets (other than Intellectual Property, which is addressed in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.25</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">) the use or benefit of which are reasonably necessary and sufficient for the operation of the Business as currently conducted.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700876"></a><a name="_Ref439971898"></a>4.12<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Contracts</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052697"></a><a name="_Ref439129039"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.12(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule sets forth a true and complete list of all of the following Contracts to which (i) any Acquired Company is a party or by which any Acquired Company or its properties or other assets are otherwise bound and (ii) the Project Development Company is a party with respect to the Acquired Assets or by which any Acquired Asset is otherwise bound (each, a &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Material Contract</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;):</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">loan agreements, credit agreements, sale-leaseback agreements, security agreements, indentures and other Contracts that provide for (A) the borrowing of moneys by or extensions of credit to any Acquired Company or to the Project Development Company with respect to the Acquired Assets by any other Person, (B) the guaranty by any Acquired Company of obligations in respect of the borrowings of money by or extensions of credit to any other Person, (C) the guaranty by Parent or any of its Affiliates (other than any Acquired Company) of obligations of any Acquired Company or with respect to the Acquired Assets or (D) reimbursement agreements relating to guarantees;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">27</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">commodity, currency or interest rate hedge, exchange or similar agreements;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">partnership, shareholder, joint venture, joint development or limited liability company agreements or other agreements setting forth arrangements between the members or partners thereto;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iv)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">power purchase, sale or exchange agreements (including sales of capacity, energy, ancillary services or related attributes or renewable energy credits or renewable attributes);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(v)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(A) electricity interconnection agreements and (B) transmission agreements;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(vi)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(A) engineering, procurement and construction agreements, (B) equipment supply agreements, (C) warranty agreements and performance guarantee agreements and (D) operation and maintenance agreements;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(vii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">labor agreements, collective bargaining agreements or similar agreements with any union, works council or similar body;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(viii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">non-competition, non-interference, non-solicitation, exclusivity or similar agreements which restrict the ability of any Acquired Company to engage in any line of business, acquire any property, develop or distribute any product, provide any service (including geographic restrictions) or to compete with any Person, in any market, field or territory;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ix)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">agreements (other than any Transaction Document) between (I) Parent or any of its Affiliates (excluding the Acquired Companies), on the one hand, and (II) any of the Acquired Companies, on the other hand;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(x)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">agreements (other than any Transaction Document) between (I) Parent or any of its Affiliates (excluding the Project Development Company), on the one hand, and (II) the Project Development Company, on the other hand, which relate to the Acquired Assets;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(xi)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">leases, subleases and any other material agreements affecting, benefiting, or burdening all or any part of the Real Property Interests;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(xii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">agreements subjecting any Acquired Company to any obligation or requirement to provide for or to make any investment in, any Person; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(xiii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">any agreement, other than those set forth in the foregoing clauses (i) through (xii), which expressly provides for future payment (A) to or from, or Liabilities of, any Acquired Company or (B) with respect to any Acquired Asset, of at least $350,000 over the term of such Contract.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">28</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052698"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.12(b)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there is no material default (i) on the part of the Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company, as applicable, or (ii) to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, on the part of any other Person, in each case, under any Material Contract.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Project Development Company and each Acquired Company and, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, each other Person, in each case, has complied in all material respects with, and is in compliance in all material respects with, the provisions of each Material Contract to which it is a party.</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052699"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each Material Contract constitutes a legal, valid and binding obligation of the Project Development Company and each Acquired Company party thereto (and, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, each other Person party thereto), and is in full force and effect and enforceable against the Project Development Company or the Acquired Company party thereto (and, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, each other Person party thereto) in accordance with its terms (except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, insolvency, reorganization, moratorium or similar Laws relating to or affecting the enforcement of creditors&#8217; rights in general and by general principles of equity). </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052700"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.12(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, Parent has made available to Purchaser true, complete and correct copies of all Material Contracts (including all written amendments, modifications, extensions and renewals thereof and related notices and agreements thereto).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439134589"></a><a name="_Toc439700877"></a>4.13<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Compliance With Laws</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. The Acquired Companies are in compliance, in all material respects, with all material Laws.&nbsp;&nbsp;With respect to the Acquired Assets, the Project Development Company is in compliance, in all material respects, with all material Laws.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.13</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no material investigations by any Governmental Entity pending or, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, threatened against the Acquired Companies or any Phase 1(a) Assets or Acquired Assets and, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, there are no facts or circumstances that will give rise to a material investigation by a Governmental Entity against the Acquired Companies or any Phase 1(a) Assets or Acquired Assets.&nbsp;&nbsp;Neither Parent nor its Affiliates nor any Acquired Company has received any written communication from any Governmental Entity that alleges that any Acquired Company, any Phase 1(a) Asset or any Acquired Asset is not in compliance, in any material respect, with any material Law which has not been resolved.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700878"></a><a name="_Ref439971907"></a>4.14<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Permits</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052703"></a><a name="_Ref439129078"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as noted on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.14</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, (i) the Project Development Company and the applicable Acquired Companies own or otherwise hold all the material Permits, including Environmental Permits, necessary to enable (A) the Project Company to own, lease or otherwise hold and operate its properties and to carry on its business as currently conducted or (B) the Project Development Company to own, lease or otherwise hold and operate the Acquired Assets, in each case including all Permits required to be obtained under Law, including Environmental Law, relating to the development, construction, operation, ownership and maintenance of the Project (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Project Permits</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;), (ii) each such Project Permit is valid and in full force and effect, and (iii) neither the Project Development Company nor any Acquired Company is in material violation of, and, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, no </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">29</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">condition exists that with notice or lapse of time or both would constitute a material violation of, any Project Permit.</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052704"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">None of Parent, AssetCo, their Affiliates, the Project Development Company or the Acquired Companies have received any written communication that any Governmental Entity intends to revoke, cancel or terminate, or to amend in a manner materially adverse to the interests of the Acquired Companies or the Acquired Assets, any such Project Permit.&nbsp;&nbsp;True and correct copies of each such Project Permit (including all written amendments, modifications, extensions and renewals thereof and related notices and agreements thereof) that has been obtained or made by or for the benefit of the Acquired Companies or the Acquired Assets have been made available to Purchaser.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439136855"></a><a name="_Ref439137135"></a><a name="_Ref439137168"></a><a name="_Toc439700879"></a>4.15<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Taxes</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except as noted on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.15</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052706"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">the Acquired Companies are treated and have always been treated, for U.S. federal income Tax purposes as either (i) a partnership, and are not treated and have not been treated, as a corporation or a &#8220;publicly traded partnership&#8221; (within the meaning of Section 7704 of the Code) taxable as a corporation, or (ii) an entity disregarded as separate from its owner as described in Treasury Regulation &#167; 301.7701-3;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052707"></a><a name="_Ref441096748"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">the Acquired Companies have, and, with respect to the Acquired Assets, the Project Development Company has, timely filed or, in the event not so timely filed, filed without material tax consequences for being untimely, all Tax Returns (other than immaterial Tax Returns for Taxes other than income Taxes) required to be filed by or with respect to it, and all such filed Tax Returns are true, complete and correct in all material respects;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052708"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">the Acquired Companies have, and, with respect to the Acquired Assets, the Project Development Company has, (i)&#160;paid all Taxes shown as due on any Tax Return, and (ii)&#160;withheld or collected and deposited with, or paid over to, the appropriate Governmental Entities all Taxes required by applicable law to be withheld or collected by it;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052709"></a>(d)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">none of AssetCo, the Project Development Company or the Acquired Companies have received from any Governmental Entity any written notice of a proposed adjustment, deficiency or underpayment of any Taxes, which notice has not been satisfied by payment or withdrawn, and there are no claims that have been asserted or threatened relating to any Taxes against or with respect to the Acquired Assets or the Acquired Companies, as applicable;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052710"></a><a name="_Ref439971915"></a>(e)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">there is no present, pending or threatened Action by any Governmental Entity for the assessment or collection of any Tax payable by or with respect to the Phase 1(a) Assets, the Acquired Assets or the Business;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052711"></a><a name="_Ref439971918"></a><a name="_Ref441096778"></a>(f)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">neither AssetCo nor the Acquired Companies nor any of their Affiliates has waived or agreed to any extension of any statute of limitations or period of limitations for any Taxes of or with respect to the Phase 1(a) Assets, the Acquired Assets or the Business that is currently in effect;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">30</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052712"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(g)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Governmental Entity in a jurisdiction where an Acquired Company does not file a Tax Return has made a claim or assertion or threatened that such Acquired Company is or may be subject to Tax in such jurisdiction;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052713"></a>(h)<font style="margin-left:0pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">there are no Tax rulings, requests for rulings, or closing agreements for or on behalf of the Acquired Companies which could affect the liability for Taxes of the Acquired Companies;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052714"></a>(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">none of AssetCo, the Project Development Company or the Acquired Companies are or have ever been a party to any &#8220;listed transaction&#8221; as defined in Treasury Regulations Section 1.6011-4(b)(2);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052715"></a>(j)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">none of the assets held by an Acquired Company is &#8220;tax-exempt use property&#8221; within the meaning of Section 168(h) of the Code or subject to the alternative depreciation system under Section 168(g) of the Code;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052716"></a><a name="_Ref439971924"></a>(k)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">there are no Liens (other than Permitted Liens) or encumbrances for Taxes on the Company Interests or upon any Phase 1(a) Assets or the Acquired Assets;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052717"></a>(l)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Cash Grant has been applied for or received with respect to the Project or the Acquired Companies;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052718"></a>(m)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">neither Parent nor any of its Affiliates nor any of the Acquired Companies has received any written notification, and Parent does not otherwise have Knowledge, of any fact, event, condition or circumstance that could be expected to result in a reallocation, recapture or denial of any Project Tax Credit with respect to the Project or the Acquired Companies;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052719"></a>(n)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, all Tax Returns for which any Project Tax Credit has been claimed have been timely filed in accordance with applicable law and all such filings are true, correct and complete in all material respects; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052720"></a>(o)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">the Acquired Companies are not a party to any Tax sharing, Tax indemnification or similar agreement, other than customary Tax indemnification provisions contained in the Material Contracts.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700880"></a><a name="_Ref439971930"></a>4.16<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Litigation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except as disclosed on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.16</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no material Actions pending or, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, threatened (and to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge as of the Execution Date, there are no facts or circumstances that will give rise to a material Action) against any Acquired Company, any Acquired Asset or the Project, or any current or former member, director or officer of any Acquired Company acting in such capacity.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.16</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, there are no outstanding Orders to which any Acquired Company is a party, or by which any Acquired Company or any Phase 1(a) Asset or Acquired Asset is bound by or with any Governmental Entity, except any such Order that is not material and that does not challenge or seek to prevent, enjoin or otherwise delay the transactions contemplated in this Agreement and in the other Transaction Documents.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">31</p>
