<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700881"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">4.17</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Absence of Material Adverse Effect</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> From and after January 3, 2016,&#160;there has not been any event, circumstance, condition or change that, individually or in the aggregate, has had a Parent Material Adverse Effect.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700882"></a><a name="_Ref440110520"></a>4.18<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Insurance</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. The Acquired Companies carry or are entitled to the benefits of insurance, with financially sound and reputable insurers, in such amounts and covering such risks as is available on commercially reasonable terms and generally maintained by companies engaged in the same or similar business and owning similar properties in the same general areas and in similar stages of development or operation, as applicable.&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule&#160;4.18</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, all such insurance policies carried by or maintained for the benefit of the Acquired Companies (the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Insurance Policies</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) are in full force and effect, all premiums in respect of such insurance have been paid in full when and as due and there is no material claim by or on behalf of any Acquired Company pending under any such policies as to which coverage has been denied or disputed by the underwriters of such policies.&nbsp;&nbsp;No notice of cancellation or non-renewal of any Insurance Policy, or any material changes that are required in the conduct of the Acquired Companies as a condition to the continuation of coverage under or renewal of any such Insurance Policy, has been received by Parent or any Acquired Company or their Affiliates.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700883"></a><a name="_Toc438052725"></a>4.19<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Employees; Employee Benefits</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="_Toc438052725"></a>.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The Acquired Companies do not have, and since their formation have not ever had, any employees.&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Acquired Company is not a party to nor bound by, and since its formation has never been party to nor bound by, any collective bargaining agreements or any other labor-related agreements with any labor union or labor organization.&nbsp;&nbsp;There are no strikes, lockouts, work stoppages, slowdowns or other material labor disputes against or affecting, in any material respect, any Acquired Company or Project.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052726"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">No Acquired Company maintains, sponsors, contributes to or is required to contribute to any Plan.&nbsp;&nbsp;There does not exist now, nor do any circumstances exist that reasonably could be expected to result in any Liability of any of the Acquired Companies with respect to any Plan now maintained or previously maintained by any of the Acquired Companies or any ERISA Affiliate of any of the Acquired Companies (or to which such an entity ever contributed or was required to contribute).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439139971"></a><a name="_Toc439700884"></a><a name="_Toc438052728"></a>4.20<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Environmental Matters</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.20(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule and for such matters that would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Parent Material Adverse Effect:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(A) no Environmental Claim is pending, or to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, threatened against any of the Acquired Companies or the Acquired Assets, and (B) to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, there are no actions, activities, circumstances, facts, conditions, events or incidents that would be reasonably likely to form the basis of any Environmental Claim against any of the Acquired Companies or the Acquired Assets; </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">32</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">(A) there is no contamination of, and there have been no Releases or threatened Releases of Hazardous Substances at any Real Property Interest or, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, on any real property formerly owned, leased or operated by any of the Acquired Companies (or any of their predecessors), and (B) to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, there are no underground storage tanks, surface impoundments, pits or lagoons in which Hazardous Substances are being or have been treated, stored, or disposed, that in the case of either (A) or (B) could reasonably be expected to give rise to an Environmental Claim against any of the Acquired Companies or the Acquired Assets; and</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">the Project Development Company with respect to the Acquired Assets and the Acquired Companies are in compliance with all Environmental Laws and all Environmental Permits, and there are no Liabilities under Environmental Laws with respect to (A) the Acquired Companies or (B) the Project Development Company with respect to the Acquired Assets.&nbsp;&nbsp;All notices, permits, permit exemptions, licenses or similar authorizations, if any, required to be obtained or filed by AssetCo, the Acquired Companies or the Project Development Company under any Environmental Laws in connection with its current assets, operations and business have been duly obtained or filed, are valid and currently in effect.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052729"></a><a name="_Ref439129415"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="_Ref439129415"></a>Parent has delivered to, or has otherwise made available for inspection by Purchaser, true, complete and correct copies of all material written reports of environmental investigations, studies, audits and tests in the possession, control or custody of Parent, AssetCo, their Affiliates, the Project Development Company or any Acquired Company relating to Environmental Laws or the Release or threatened Release of Hazardous Substances at, in, on, under or from any Real Property Interests.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439141699"></a><a name="_Toc439700885"></a>4.21<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">No Brokers</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.21</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, none of Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company or the Acquired Companies or any of their Affiliates has authorized any Person to act as broker, finder or in any other similar capacity in connection with the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and the negotiations leading to it which will have a right of payment or claim against Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company or any of its Affiliates, or against any Acquired Company.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700886"></a><a name="_Toc438052733"></a>4.22<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Regulation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"><a name="_Toc438052733"></a>. Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.22</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, the Project Company either (A) has received MBR Authority and status as an EWG, or (B) if the Project Company has not received MBR Authority and status as an EWG, (I) to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, there is no reason why the Project Company would not receive MBR Authority or be eligible for status as an EWG, in each case, prior to the first delivery or sale of Electricity from the Project, and (II) are not, and prior to the earlier of (x) the date of FERC&#8217;s order granting it MBR Authority or (y) the effective date of its MBR Authority, will not be, subject to regulation as a &#8220;public utility&#8221; under the FPA or subject to regulation under PUHCA.&nbsp;&nbsp;Each of the Acquired Companies is either not subject to or is exempt from regulation as a &#8220;public utility,&#8221; &#8220;electric utility,&#8221; &#8220;electric corporation,&#8221; or similar term under the public utility laws and regulations of any state.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">33</p>

<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700887"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">4.23</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Related Party Transactions</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> Except for Material Contracts or as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.23</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule:</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052735"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">neither Parent nor any Affiliate thereof (other than the Acquired Companies) is a party to, or is subject to, any Contract entered into by any Acquired Company; </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052736"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Phase 1(a) Asset is owned or controlled by Parent or any Affiliate thereof (other than any Acquired Company), other than indirectly by virtue of its ownership interest in any Acquired Company; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">following the Phase 1(b) Closing and the Phase 2 Closing, no Phase 1(b) Asset or Phase 2 Asset, as applicable, will be owned or controlled by Parent or any Affiliate thereof (other than any Acquired Company), other than indirectly by virtue of its ownership interest in any Acquired Company.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129498"></a><a name="_Toc439700888"></a>4.24<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Credit Support</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.24</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule sets forth a list of all currently effective letters of credit, guarantees, deposits and other credit support provided by or on behalf of Parent or its Affiliates to or on behalf of any Acquired Company or Acquired Asset relating to the ownership and operation of the Project or as required pursuant to any Material Contract or Project Permit.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439139970"></a><a name="_Toc439700889"></a><a name="_Toc438052739"></a>4.25<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Intellectual Property</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Except as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 4.25(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule, (i) the Acquired Companies own, free and clear of any Liens other than Permitted Liens, or have the licenses or rights to use for the Business, and (ii) the Project Development Company owns, free and clear of any Liens other than Permitted Liens, or has the licenses or rights to use with respect to the Acquired Assets, all material Intellectual Property currently used in the Business as currently conducted or with respect to the Acquired Assets, as applicable, and the consummation of transactions contemplated by the Transaction Documents will not adversely alter or impair any such right in any material respect; </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">provided</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">however</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, the foregoing and the representation in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.13</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> shall not be deemed to constitute a representation or warranty with respect to infringement or other violation of Intellectual Property rights of third Persons, which are exclusively addressed below in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.25(b)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052740"></a><a name="_Ref439970412"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">To Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, the use by (i) the Acquired Companies of the Intellectual Property currently used in the Business and (ii) the Acquired Assets does not infringe upon the Intellectual Property rights of any Person in any manner that would reasonably be expected to have a Parent Material Adverse Effect. </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052741"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">None of Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company or the Acquired Companies have (i) received from any Person a written or, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, unwritten claim that (A) the Acquired Companies or (B) with respect to the Acquired Assets, the Project Development Company, are infringing in any material respect the Intellectual Property of such Person or (ii) received any written or, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, unwritten, notice of any default, and, to Parent&#8217;s Knowledge, no event has occurred that with notice or lapse of time, or both, would constitute a material default under any material Intellectual Property License that would reasonably be expected to have a Parent Material Adverse Effect.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">34</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052742"></a><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(d)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company and the Acquired Companies have taken commercially reasonable measures to protect the confidentiality of all material trade secrets of the Acquired Companies or included in the Acquired Assets.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700890"></a>4.26<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Projections</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. The Financial Projections were prepared in good faith based on reasonable assumptions of Parent and are materially consistent with Parent&#8217;s current expectations regarding the Project, and the assumptions included in the Financial Projections are materially consistent with the provisions of the Contracts affecting the Project.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700891"></a>4.27<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Limitation of Representations and Warranties</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. EXCEPT FOR THE REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES SET FORTH IN THIS </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">ARTICLE IV</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, PARENT IS NOT MAKING ANY OTHER REPRESENTATIONS OR WARRANTIES, WRITTEN OR ORAL, STATUTORY, EXPRESS OR IMPLIED, CONCERNING THE ACQUIRED COMPANIES, THE COMPANY INTERESTS, THE PROJECT, OR THE ACQUIRED ASSETS, THE PHASE 1(A) ASSETS, OR THE BUSINESS OR THE LIABILITIES OF THE ACQUIRED COMPANIES, INCLUDING, IN PARTICULAR, ANY WARRANTY OF MERCHANTABILITY OR FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE, ALL OF WHICH ARE HEREBY EXPRESSLY EXCLUDED AND DISCLAIMED.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700892"></a>ARTICLE V<font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br><br>REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES OF PURCHASER</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Purchaser hereby represents and warrants to Parent as follows as of the Execution Date:</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439128692"></a><a name="_Toc439700893"></a>5.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Organization; Qualification</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052749"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each of Purchaser and 8point3 OpCo Holdings has been duly formed and is validly existing and in good standing as a limited liability company under the Laws of its jurisdiction of formation</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">with all requisite limited liability company power and authority to own, lease or otherwise hold and operate its properties and assets and to carry on its business as presently conducted, except in each case where the failure to have such power and authority would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Purchaser Material Adverse Effect.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052750"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each of Purchaser and 8point3 OpCo Holdings is duly qualified and in good standing to do business as a foreign limited liability company in each jurisdiction in which the conduct or nature of its business or the ownership, leasing, holding or operating of its properties makes such qualification necessary, except such jurisdictions where the failure to be so qualified or in good standing would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Purchaser Material Adverse Effect.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052751"></a>(c)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Purchaser has heretofore made available to Parent complete and correct copies of the Charter Documents of each of Purchaser and 8point3 OpCo Holdings.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439128699"></a><a name="_Toc439700894"></a>5.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Authority and Power</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Each of Purchaser and 8point3 OpCo Holdings (a) has all requisite limited liability company power and authority to execute and deliver the Transaction Documents to which it is a party, to perform its obligations hereunder and thereunder, and to </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">35</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">consummate the transactions contemplated hereby and thereby, and (b) has taken all necessary limited liability company action to authorize the execution, delivery and performance of the Transaction Documents to which it is a party.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439128710"></a><a name="_Toc439700895"></a>5.03<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Valid and Binding Obligation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052754"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">This Agreement has been duly and validly executed and delivered by Purchaser and, assuming this Agreement has been duly and validly authorized, executed and delivered by Parent, constitutes a legal, valid and binding obligation of Purchaser, enforceable against Purchaser in accordance with its terms, except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, insolvency, fraudulent transfer, reorganization, moratorium or similar Laws relating to or affecting the enforcement of creditors&#8217; rights in general and by general principles of equity.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc438052755"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Each of the Transaction Documents to which Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings is a party will be duly and validly executed and delivered by Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings, as applicable, and, upon execution and delivery thereof, and assuming such Transaction Document has been duly and validly authorized, executed and delivered by each Parent Party that will be a party thereto, will constitute a legal, valid and binding obligation of Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings, as applicable, enforceable against Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings, as applicable, in accordance with its terms, except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, insolvency, fraudulent transfer, reorganization, moratorium or similar Laws relating to or affecting the enforcement of creditors&#8217; rights in general and by general principles of equity.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700896"></a>5.04<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">No Violation or Conflict</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. None of the execution, delivery or performance of this Agreement or any of the other Transaction Documents by Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings, nor the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby or thereby, will (a) conflict with or violate any provision of the Charter Documents of Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings, (b) constitute, with or without notice or the passage of time or both, a Default under any material Permit or Contract to which Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings is a party or by which any of their respective properties are bound, or (c) contravene, in any material respect, any material Law.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700897"></a>5.05<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Consents and Approvals</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. No material Consent of, with or to any Governmental Entity or other Person is required to be obtained or made by or with respect to Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings in connection with the execution and delivery of this Agreement and the other Transaction Documents, or the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby or thereby.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439128676"></a><a name="_Toc439700898"></a>5.06<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">No Brokers</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Neither Purchaser nor any of its Affiliates has authorized any Person to act as broker, finder or in any other similar capacity in connection with the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and the negotiations leading to it which will have a right of payment or claim against Parent, AssetCo, the Project Development Company or any of their Affiliates.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc436051597"></a><a name="_Toc436051704"></a><a name="_Toc436051783"></a><a name="_Ref436051954"></a><a name="_Toc436768404"></a><a name="_Toc439700899"></a><a name="_Toc436051168"></a><a name="_Ref436051955"></a>5.07<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Litigation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. There are no outstanding Orders to which Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings is a party, or by which Purchaser or 8point3 OpCo Holdings is bound by or with any </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">36</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Governmental Entity, except any such Order that does not challenge or seek to prevent, enjoin or otherwise delay the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and by the other Transaction Documents.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700900"></a><a name="_Toc438052856"></a>5.08<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Investment Intent</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.<a name="_Toc438052856"></a> Purchaser is acquiring the Company Interests for its own account with the present intention of holding the Company Interests for investment purposes and not with a view to, or for offer or sale in connection with, any distribution thereof in violation of the Securities Act or state securities laws. The Partnership, Purchaser and 8point3 OpCo Holdings acknowledge that the Company Interests will not be registered under the Securities Act or any applicable state securities law, and that such Company Interests may not be transferred or sold except pursuant to the registration provisions of the Securities Act or pursuant to an applicable exemption therefrom and pursuant to state securities laws and regulations as applicable.&nbsp;&nbsp;Purchaser is an &#8220;accredited investor&#8221; as defined under Rule 501 promulgated under the Securities Act.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439136881"></a><a name="_Toc439700901"></a>5.09<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Disqualified Person</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Purchaser is not a Disqualified Person.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700902"></a>5.10<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Limitation of Representations and Warranties</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. EXCEPT FOR THE REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES SET FORTH IN THIS </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">ARTICLE V</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, PURCHASER IS NOT MAKING ANY OTHER REPRESENTATIONS OR WARRANTIES CONCERNING THE TRANSACTIONS CONTEMPLATED BY THIS AGREEMENT, WRITTEN OR ORAL, STATUTORY, EXPRESS OR IMPLIED.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700903"></a>ARTICLE VI<font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br><br>COVENANTS</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref441099765"></a><a name="_Ref441100434"></a><a name="_Ref441100683"></a>6.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Conduct of Business Prior to the Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref408065678"></a><a name="_Ref394687234"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Between the date of this Agreement and the earlier of the termination of this Agreement in accordance with its terms and the applicable Closing Date (such period, the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Interim Period</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;), except (i) as otherwise expressly contemplated by this Agreement, (ii) as required by Law, (iii) as set forth on </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule 6.01(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> of the Parent Disclosure Schedule (such scheduled matters, the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Permitted Interim Actions</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;), (iv) as required by or pursuant to any Material Contract or Project Permit, (v) as required by the Tax Equity Financing, or (vi) with the prior written consent of the Purchaser (which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld, delayed, or conditioned), Parent shall in good faith, subject to any applicable requirements set forth in the Charter Documents of the Project Development Company, (A) cause its Subsidiaries to vote their respective Equity Interests in the Project Development Company, as applicable, and (B) otherwise exercise all rights and powers available to it to cause the Project Development Company:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">to use commercially reasonable efforts to (A) maintain all of the Acquired Assets, including the Real Property Interests and the Project Permits thereof, in accordance with Prudent Solar Industry Practices and (B) to the extent applicable, pursue the continued construction and development of the </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">37</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Development Project Sites in accordance with all applicable Project Permits and Material Contracts included in the Acquired Assets;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">not to make any material change in the conduct of its business as it relates to the Acquired Assets;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">not to contribute any of the Acquired Assets to any partnership or joint venture;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iv)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">except as permitted by exclusions under other clauses of this </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 6.01(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> and other than in the ordinary course of business, not to enter into any Material Contract included in the Acquired Assets or terminate, amend or breach in any material respect any Material Contract included in the Acquired Assets to which it is a party or waive any material rights under any Material Contract included in the Acquired Assets to which it is a party, except for amendments to the power purchase agreements and site leases included in the Acquired Assets only to the extent necessary to adjust the number of Development Project Sites included in the Phase 1(b) Closing and the Phase 2 Closing; provided, however, that such amendments do not change the financial terms of such power purchase or site lease agreements;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(v)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">not to incur, assume or guarantee any Indebtedness on the Acquired Assets;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(vi)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">not to sell, assign, transfer, abandon, lease or otherwise dispose of Acquired Assets having a fair market value in excess of $250,000 in the aggregate, except for (1) capacity, energy, ancillary services or related attributes in the ordinary course of business and documented by a Material Contract or (2) dispositions of inventory or worn-out or obsolete equipment for fair value in the ordinary course of business;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(vii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">other than Permitted Liens, not to grant any security interest with respect to, pledge or otherwise encumber any Acquired Assets;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(viii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">not to settle any claims, demands, lawsuits or state or federal regulatory proceedings for damages to the extent such settlements in the aggregate assess damages against the Acquired Assets in excess of $250,000 (other than any claims, demands, lawsuits or proceedings to the extent insured (net of deductibles), or to the extent covered by an indemnity obligation not subject to dispute or adjustment from a solvent indemnitor);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ix)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">except as (A) required on an emergency basis or for the safety of persons or the environment or (B) in accordance with the Material Contracts, not to make any capital expenditure in excess of $250,000 in the aggregate;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(x)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">not to make, amend or revoke any Tax elections, change or consent to any change in any method of accounting for any Tax purpose, enter </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">38</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">into any closing agreement affecting any Tax liability or refund or file any request for rulings or special Tax incentives with any Governmental Entity, settle or compromise any Tax liability or refund, or extend or waive the application of any statute of limitations regarding the assessment or collection of any Tax, in each case to the extent related to the Acquired Assets;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(xi)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">fail to file on a timely basis all applications and other documents necessary to maintain, renew or extend any Project Permit or any other material Permit required by any Governmental Entity for the continuing operation of the Acquired Assets; or</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(xii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">agree or commit to do any of the foregoing.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Notwithstanding any provision in this <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.01</font> to the contrary, the restrictions set forth in this <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.01</font> shall apply only to the business, operations, agreements, indebtedness and securities included in the Acquired Assets and shall not apply to the business, operations, agreements, indebtedness and securities of, or otherwise restrict the activities of, Parent or any of its Affiliates.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref441100691"></a>(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">During the Interim Period, Parent shall promptly notify Purchaser in writing of:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">any event, condition or circumstance that could reasonably be expected to result in any of the conditions set forth in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Article VII</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> not being satisfied on or prior to the applicable Closing Date; </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">any change, event or occurrence that has had or could reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect; </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">any material breach by Parent of any covenant, obligation or agreement contained in this Agreement; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iv)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">any Material Contract entered into or amended during the Interim Period, and Parent shall make available a true, correct and complete copy of such Contract or amendment thereto (as applicable);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">provided</font> that the delivery of any notice pursuant to this <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.01(b)</font> shall not limit or otherwise affect the remedies available hereunder of Purchaser or the conditions set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Article VII</font>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700904"></a><a name="_Toc439700905"></a>6.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Further Assurances</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. In the event that at any time after any Closing any further action is necessary to carry out the purposes of the Transaction Documents, each of the Parties shall take such further action (including the execution and delivery of such further documents and instruments) as the other Party may reasonably request, all at the sole expense of the requesting Party (unless the action requested should have been taken prior to such Closing, in which case the Party that would have borne the expense of taking such action had it been taken prior to such Closing shall bear such expense).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">39</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">6.03</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Post-Closing Delivery Obligations</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. After each of the Phase 1(b) Closing and the Phase 2 Closing, Parent shall deliver, or cause to be delivered, to Purchaser, the Payment Request and the Tax Equity Funds Flow, in each case, with respect to the Subsequent Tranche Payment Date (as defined in the Master Purchase Agreement) for such Closing.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">6.04<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Expenses</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Except as otherwise provided in this Agreement, all costs and expenses incurred in connection with this Agreement shall be paid by the Party incurring such expenses.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700906"></a>6.05<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Amended and Restated Omnibus Agreement</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Within two (2) months following the Execution Date, Purchaser will use commercially reasonable efforts to (a) obtain approval to enter into the Amended and Restated Omnibus Agreement from the lenders under the Credit Agreement and (b) execute the Amended and Restated Omnibus Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;Upon the execution of the Amended and Restated Omnibus Agreement, (y) the following provisions of this Agreement will automatically terminate and be of no further force or effect: (i) clauses (ii) and (iii) of the definition of &#8220;Parent Indemnified Taxes,&#8221; (ii) </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Sections 10.05</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, 10.07 and </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">10.08</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> and (iii) any definitions used exclusively therein, and (z) this Agreement will automatically be amended to replace the form of Omnibus Agreement Amendment attached hereto as Exhibit B with a form of Omnibus Agreement Amendment that (I) replaces Section 1.05 of the form of Omnibus Agreement Amendment with the words &#8220;Intentionally Omitted&#8221;, and (II) makes such changes as are necessary or appropriate to indicate that it is an amendment to the Amended and Restated Omnibus Agreement.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439978998"></a>6.06<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule Update</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref441322290"></a>(a)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Three (3) Business Days prior to each of the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date and the Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date, Parent shall deliver to Purchaser a true and complete schedule of changes (each, a &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Schedule Update</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) to any of the information contained in the Parent Disclosure Schedule with respect to the Phase 1(b) Assets or the Phase 2 Assets, as applicable (including changes to any other representation or warranty in Article IV as to which no Schedule has been created as of the date hereof but as to which a Schedule would have been required hereunder to have been created on or before the Execution Date if such changes had existed on the Execution Date), which changes are required as a result of events or circumstances occurring subsequent to the Execution Date which would render any Parent Bringdown Representation inaccurate or incomplete at the applicable Closing Date.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Any information disclosed in any Schedule Update shall not be deemed to have cured any inaccuracy in or breach of any representation or warranty contained in this Agreement (including any representation or warranty included in any Closing Certificate), including for purposes of the indemnification or termination rights contained in this Agreement or of determining whether or not the conditions set forth in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 7.01(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> or </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 7.02(a)</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> have been satisfied.&nbsp;&nbsp;For avoidance of doubt, Purchaser&#8217;s knowledge of any breach of any representation or warranty prior to any Closing as a result of any Schedule Update shall not affect any liability on the part of Parent pursuant to this Agreement (including any Closing Certificate).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">40</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">6.07</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Commercial Operation</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Parent shall, and shall cause its Affiliates to, take all commercially reasonable actions necessary to ensure that the Phase 1(b) Assets and the Phase 2 Assets achieve mechanical completion on or prior to the Termination Date.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700907"></a>ARTICLE VII<font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br><br>CONDITIONS TO CLOSING</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">7.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Conditions to Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. (a) The obligations of Purchaser to consummate the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing is subject to the satisfaction or waiver, at or prior to the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing, of the following conditions:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent shall have delivered, or cause to be delivered, the Tranche Presentation Certificate with respect to the closing of Phase 1(b) to Purchaser;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent shall have delivered, or cause to be delivered, the CP and Funding Acknowledgement with respect to the closing of Phase 1(b) to Purchaser;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Law shall be in effect and no Order shall have been entered or issued, in each case that restrains, enjoins or prohibits the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iv)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">between the Execution Date and the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date, no Parent Material Adverse Effect shall have occurred with respect to the Phase 1(b) Assets.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The obligations of Parent to consummate the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing is subject to the satisfaction or waiver, at or prior to the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing, of the following conditions:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Law shall be in effect and no Order shall have been entered or issued, in each case that restrains, enjoins or prohibits the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">between the Execution Date and the Phase 1(b) Contribution Closing Date, no Purchaser Material Adverse Effect shall have occurred.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">7.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Conditions to Phase 2 Contribution Closing</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. (a) The obligations of Purchaser to consummate the Phase 2 Contribution Closing is subject to the satisfaction or waiver, at or prior to the Phase 2 Contribution Closing, of the following conditions:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent shall have delivered, or cause to be delivered, the Tranche Presentation Certificate with respect to the closing of Phase 2 to Purchaser;</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">41</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Parent shall have delivered, or cause to be delivered, the CP and Funding Acknowledgement with respect to the closing of Phase 2 to Purchaser;</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Law shall be in effect and no Order shall have been entered or issued, in each case that restrains, enjoins or prohibits the Phase 2 Contribution Closing; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(iv)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">between the Execution Date and the Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date, no Parent Material Adverse Effect shall have occurred with respect to the Phase 2 Assets.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(b)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">The obligations of Parent to consummate the Phase 2 Contribution Closing is subject to the satisfaction or waiver, at or prior to the Phase 2 Contribution Closing, of the following conditions:</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(i)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">no Law shall be in effect and no Order shall have been entered or issued, in each case that restrains, enjoins or prohibits the Phase 2 Contribution Closing; and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;margin-right:7.69%;text-indent:15.38%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">(ii)<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">between the Execution Date and the Phase 2 Contribution Closing Date, no Purchaser Material Adverse Effect shall have occurred.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">ARTICLE VIII<font style="font-family:Times New Roman Bold;color:#000000;"><br><br>SURVIVAL AND INDEMNIFICATION</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Toc439700908"></a>8.01<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Survival of Representations, Warranties and Agreements</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. The representations, warranties, covenants and agreements contained in this Agreement (including any representations, warranties, covenants or agreements included in any Closing Certificate) shall survive each Closing; </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">provided</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">however</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">, an Indemnified Party may bring a claim for or with respect to inaccuracy or breach of any representation or warranty only if it has notified the Indemnifying Party of the breach on or before the date that is eighteen (18) months after the applicable Closing Date on which such representation or warranty was made, except that claims for or with respect to any inaccuracy or breach of (a) any Specified Representation shall survive indefinitely, (b) any representation or warranty contained in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.20</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> (</font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Environmental Matters</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">) shall survive each Closing until the date that is three (3) years after the applicable Closing Date on which such representation or warranty was made, and (c) any representation or warranty contained in </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Section 4.15</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;"> (</font><font style="font-style:italic;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Taxes</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">) shall survive each Closing until the date that is sixty (60) days after the expiration of the applicable statute of limitations for such representation or warranty (including any valid extensions with respect thereto).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129096"></a><a name="_Ref439137115"></a><a name="_Ref439137190"></a><a name="_Ref439137209"></a><a name="_Toc439700909"></a>8.02<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Indemnification by Parent</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">. Subject to the other terms and limitations set forth in this Agreement, Parent agrees to indemnify, defend and hold harmless Purchaser, Purchaser&#8217;s Affiliates and each of their respective Representatives (collectively, the &#8220;</font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">Purchaser Group</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">&#8221;) from and against any and all Damages incurred or sustained by any member of the Purchaser Group to the extent arising out of, relating to or resulting from (a) any failure by Parent to perform any </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">42</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">covenant or agreement of Parent contained in this Agreement, and (b) any inaccuracy or breach of any of Parent&#8217;s representations and warranties contained in this Agreement.</font>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.69%;color:#000000;font-family:9999999;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_Ref439129295"></a><a name="_Ref439137121"></a><a name="_Ref439137197"></a><a name="_Ref439137216"></a><a name="_Toc439700910"></a>8.03<font style="margin-left:36pt;"></font><font style="text-decoration:underline;font-family:Times New Roman;">Indemnification by Purchaser</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">.
